Gang Seol spent 25 years living a mundane, lonely life as an orphan, but every night for 17 years, he escaped into the 'World of Eternity. While others saw him as a crazy loner, he was secretly mastering a world that was more real to him than his own poverty-stricken reality. When the 'trial version' of his dreams ended, the unthinkable happened: the game merged with reality. Betrayed and fueled by a lifetime of isolation, Gang Seol—known in the game as 'Snowman'—refuses to be a pawn any longer.
